---

This is a self-contained version of some solutions for HoTT-Book's exercises.
The idea is to unpackage all as long as possible to get a better understanding.
Many changes can appear running this experiment. Solutions are
type-checked as a whole using Agda v2.5.3.

## Requirements

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="562" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="566" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="574" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="586" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Equality type definition also called Identity type:

## Chapter 1

### Exercise 1.1

{: .exercise}
  Given functions $$f : A \to B$$ and $$g:B\to C$$, define
  their composite $$ g\circ f:A\to C$$.
  Show that we have $$h \circ (g\circ f) \equiv (h\circ g)\circ f$$.


We define the composition operation in Agda as follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="_∘_"></a><a id="2159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2159" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a> <a id="2163" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2165" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2167" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2168" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="2170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2170" class="Bound">j</a> <a id="2172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2172" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2173" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2175" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2176" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2178" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2180" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2168" class="Bound">i</a><a id="2185" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2187" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2187" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2189" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2191" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2170" class="Bound">j</a><a id="2196" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="2198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2198" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="2200" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2202" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#2172" class="Bound">k</a><a id="2207" class="Symbol">}</a>

### Exercise 1.2

<div class="exercise">
Derive the recursion principle for products $$\mathsf{rec}_{A\times B}$$
using only the projections, and verify that the definitional equalities
are valid. Do the same for $$\Sigma$$-types.
</div>

To solve this problem we need to know:

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}
      : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) → A \times B \to C.
    $$
    </p>

  - The recursion principle for Σ-types:

    <p class="equation">
    $$ \mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}
      : \prod\limits_{(C : U)} (\Pi_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C) \rightarrow
        \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \rightarrow C
    $$
    </p>

<div class="proof" id="proof-1.2">
Proof.<br/>
For products:<br/>
If we have the projections,
$$\mathsf{proj}_1 : A \times B \to \mathsf{A}$$ and $$\mathsf{proj}_2 : A \times B \to \mathsf{B}$$,
then $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$ is another inhabitant where

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&\mathsf{rec}_1 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}} (A \to B \to C) \to A \times B \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_1~C~g~c~:\equiv~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c,~\mathsf{proj}_2 c).
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{ A \times B}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_1$$.
<br/>
<br/>
For sums:<br/>
The projections are $$\mathsf{proj}_1 : \sum_{x : A}  Bx \to \mathsf{A}$$ and
$$\mathsf{proj}_2 :  \prod_{(p : \sum_{x : A}  Bx)} \to \mathsf{B} (\mathsf{proj}_1 p)$$.<br/>
By using these projections, we got another recursor defined as follows:
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{aling*}
&\mathsf{rec}_2 : \prod\limits_{C : \mathcal{U}}  (\prod_{x : A} Bx \to C) \to \sum\limits_{x : A} B x \to C\\
&\mathsf{rec}_2~C~g~c~=~g~(\mathsf{proj}_1 c)~(\mathsf{proj}_2 c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

By reflexivity, we prove the equality between $$\mathsf{rec}_{\sum\limits_{(x : A) } B(x)}$$ and $$\mathsf{rec}_2$$.
</div>

In Agda.<br>

Let's add some machinery to handle levels of the universe needed for
the following exercises including this one:

    <a id="5036" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ._,_"></a><a id="5048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
    <a id="5056" class="Keyword">field</a>
      <a id="Σ-Def₁.Σ.proj₁"></a><a id="5068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5068" class="Field">proj₁</a> <a id="5074" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5076" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4985" class="Bound">A</a>

  <a id="5103" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="5108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4976" class="Module">Σ</a> <a id="5110" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="5117" class="Comment">-- _,_ : (proj₁ : A) → B proj₁ → Σ A B.</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Its recursor with a function $$g : \prod_{(x : A)} B(x)\rightarrow C$$
that we provide.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On the other hand, the product type is just a particular case of the sigma type
when the codomain is not dependent, as we can see next by omitting the argument
in `(λ _ → B)`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="5822" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₁"></a><a id="5829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5829" class="Module">×-Def₁</a> <a id="5836" class="Keyword">where</a>

Its recursor with a function $$g : A \rightarrow B \rightarrow C$$ that we provide.

### Exercise 1.3

<p class="exercise">
Derive the induction principle for products $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$,
using only the projections and the propositional uniqueness principle
$$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$.
Verify that the definitional equalities are valid.
</p>

To solve this problem, recall the uniqueness principle (Pp. 29. HoTT-Book)

- The **propositional uniqueness principle** says that
every element of $$A\times B$$ is equal to a pair.

<p class="equation">
  $$ \mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}
     : \prod_{(x : A \times B)} ((\mathsf{proj}_{1}(x) , \mathsf{proj}_{2}(x))
       \equiv_{A\times B} x).
  $$
</p>

Product type definition using `data`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6991" class="Comment">-- this would be trivial in agda due to definitional η for records</a>
<a id="7058" class="Comment">-- so Capriotti defined a product type without η:</a>

Projections and $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7447" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Fun₂"></a><a id="7454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7454" class="Module">×-Fun₂</a> <a id="7461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7462" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7462" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7464" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7465" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7467" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7469" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7471" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7475" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7462" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7476" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7478" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="7480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7482" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="7486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7464" class="Bound">j</a><a id="7487" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7489" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="7497" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7115" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="7509" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="7515" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="7517" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7136" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="7520" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="7521" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7192" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="7524" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="7526" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="7531" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="7533" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7296" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="7538" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7543" class="Comment">-- propositional uniqueness principle:</a>

        <a id="7954" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7956" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7927" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7958" href="{% Operator">≡</a> <a id="7982" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7983" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7929" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7985"   <a id="7992" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7904" class="Function">pair=</a> <a id="7998" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#814" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8003" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#814" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8008" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#814" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The induction principle for the product type:

<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B} : \prod\limits_{C : A \times B \to \mathcal{U}}
  \left( \prod\limits_{x:A}\ \prod\limits_{y:B}\ \,C( (x,y) ) \right)
  \to \prod\limits_{x:A \times B}\ \,C(x)
$$
</p>

  <a id="8354" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="8359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7115" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="8366" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="8372" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7136" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="8376" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="8378" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7192" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="8381" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="8382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="8387" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="8388" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7296" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="8393" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="×-Ind₂.ind"></a><a id="8425" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8425" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="8429" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8431" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8433" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8434" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8434" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8435" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="8437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8437" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8439" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8324" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8443" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7136" class="Datatype Operator">×</a> <a id="8445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8335" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="8447" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8449" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="8453" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8434" class="Bound">k</a><a id="8454" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="8464" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8466" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="8468" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8468" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8470" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8324" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8473" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8475" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8475" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="8477" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8479" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8335" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8480" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8482" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8437" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="8486" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8487" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8468" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="8489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7192" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="8491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#8475" class="Bound">y</a><a id="8492" class="Symbol">))</a>

<p class="exercise">
Generalize $$\mathsf{uniq}_{A\times B}$$ to Σ-types, and do the same for
$$\Sigma$$-types, i.e. show induction and verify the definitional equality
is valid.
</p>

Σ-type definition using `data`:

Projections and uniqueness propositional principle:

  <a id="9862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9711" class="Function">ind-β</a> <a id="9868" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9868" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="9870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9870" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="9872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9872" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#9874" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="9876" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#814" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

### Exercise 1.4

<div class="exercise">
Assuming as given only the <em>iterator</em> for natural numbers
<p class="equation">
$$\mathsf{ite} : \prod\limits_{C:\mathcal{U}} C \to (C \to C) \to \mathbb{N} \to C $$
</p>
with the defining equations
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,0)               &\equiv c_0, \\
\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,\mathsf{suc}(n)) &\equiv c_s(\mathsf{ite}(C,c_0,c_s,n)),
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
derive a function having the type of the recursor $$\mathsf{rec}$$.
Show that the defining equations of the recursor hold propositionally for this
function, using the induction principle for $$\mathbb{N}$$.
</div>

To solve this problem, let us define the recursor and also the induction principle
for natural numbers. (See more details about these functions in
[Induction on Natural Numbers]({% post_url 2018-02-12-induction-on-natural-numbers %})).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10802" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Def"></a><a id="10809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10809" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="10815" class="Keyword">where</a>

Now, we define the iterator following the equations above:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11322" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ℕ-Fun"></a><a id="11329" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11329" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="11335" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="11343" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11348" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10809" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a> <a id="11354" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10829" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="11362" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11364" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10847" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="11368" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="11370" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10860" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a><a id="11373" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="11377" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="11382" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10881" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="11388" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="11394" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10908" class="Function">rec</a><a id="11398" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ℕ-Fun.ite"></a><a id="11403" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11403" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11409" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="11411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11412" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11412" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11416" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="11419" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11421" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11423" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11412" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11425" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11427" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11428" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11412" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11430" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11432" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11412" class="Bound">C</a><a id="11433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11435" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11437" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10829" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="11439" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11441" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11412" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="11445" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11403" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11449" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11451" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11454" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11454" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11457" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10847" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a>    <a id="11465" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11451" class="Bound">c₀</a>
  <a id="11472" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11403" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11476" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11478" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11481" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10860" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="11489" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11489" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11490" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="11492" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="11494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11481" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11497" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="11498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11403" class="Function">ite</a> <a id="11502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11476" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="11504" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11478" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="11507" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11481" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="11510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11489" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11511" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Then, we now can define the recursor using this `ite` by iterating over the type
`ℕ × C` (*reloading recursion*?).


<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11655" class="Comment">-- recursor</a>

           <a id="11908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11781" class="Bound">n</a><a id="11909" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, we need to establish the propositional equality between these two
definitions of recursor, i.e, between `rec` and `rec₂`. Let's use
induction to prove that.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="12099" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="ex1-4"></a><a id="12106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12106" class="Module">ex1-4</a> <a id="12112" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="12155" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10881" class="Module">ℕ-Rec</a> <a id="12166" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12172" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10908" class="Function">rec</a><a id="12176" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12180" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11032" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a> <a id="12191" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12197" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11059" class="Function">ind</a><a id="12201" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12205" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11329" class="Module">ℕ-Fun</a> <a id="12216" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12222" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11403" class="Function">ite</a><a id="12226" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11715" class="Function">rec₂</a><a id="12232" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="12237" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="12242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7115" class="Module">×-Def₂</a> <a id="12249" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="12255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7136" class="Datatype Operator">_×_</a><a id="12259" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12261" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">proj₁</a><a id="12266" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12268" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7296" class="Function">proj₂</a><a id="12273" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="12275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#7192" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="12278" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="ex1-4.proof"></a><a id="12297" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12297" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="12303" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12305" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12306" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12306" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12308" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12310" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="12313" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12315" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12315" class="Bound">c₀</a> <a id="12318" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12320" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12306" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12321" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="12323" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12323" class="Bound">cₛ</a> <a id="12326" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12328" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10829" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="12330" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12332" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12306" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="12334" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12336" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#12306" class="Bound">C</a><a id="12337" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="12347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12349" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="12351" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12352" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link ### Exercise 1.5

<div class="exercise">

Show that if we define

  $$A+B :\equiv \sum\limits_{(x : \mathbbbold{2})} \mathsf{rec}_{\mathbbbold{2}} (\mathcal{U}, A , B, x),$$

then we can give a definition of $$\ind\limits_{A + B}$$ for which the
definitional equalities holds.

</div>

To solve this problem, let us introduce the $$\mathcal{2}$$ type, that is, the
type with two constructors also called **Bool**. The constructors are also called
false and true respectively.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13349" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁"></a><a id="13356" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13356" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="13363" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13372" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚"></a><a id="13377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a> <a id="13379" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13381" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="13385" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟘"></a><a id="13395" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="13397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13399" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>
    <a id="𝟚-Def₁.𝟚.𝟙"></a><a id="13405" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="13407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13409" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


With the recursor:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13457" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="𝟚-Rec₁"></a><a id="13464" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13464" class="Module">𝟚-Rec₁</a> <a id="13471" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13480" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13485" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13356" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a>  <a id="13493" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="13499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="13501" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="13503" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="13504" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="13505" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="14263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="14267" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14267" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="14269" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14271" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="14274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14267" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14277" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Now, let's try to define the recursor for this coproduct, and later,
we'll try the dependent version of it to complete the exercise.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14439" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Rec₁"></a><a id="14446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14446" class="Module">+-Rec₁</a> <a id="14453" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="14462" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14467" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13911" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="14474" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14480" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14481" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14031" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="14484" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="14486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Function">inl</a><a id="14489" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Function">inr</a><a id="14493" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="14497" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14501" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="14506" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13356" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="14513" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="14519" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14520" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="14521" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14522" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="14523" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="14524" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="14525" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Rec₁.rec"></a><a id="14530" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14530" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14534" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14536" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14538" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14539" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="14541" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14541" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14542" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14544" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14545" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14547" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14547" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14551" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14555" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14539" class="Bound">i</a><a id="14556" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14558" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14559" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14559" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="14561" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14563" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="14567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14541" class="Bound">j</a><a id="14568" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="14576" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14545" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14581" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14583" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14559" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14584" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14592" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14595" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14547" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14597" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14559" class="Bound">C</a><a id="14600" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14608" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14545" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14031" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="14614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14547" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14616" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14559" class="Bound">C</a>
  <a id="14622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14530" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14626" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14628" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14630" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a> <a id="14633" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14635" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14635" class="Bound">a</a><a id="14636" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14638" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14640" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14626" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14635" class="Bound">a</a>
  <a id="14646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14530" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="14650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14650" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14652" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a> <a id="14657" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14659" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14659" class="Bound">b</a><a id="14660" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14662" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14664" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14652" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14659" class="Bound">b</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Notice how the recursor of the coproduct matches with the elimination
rule of the disjunction conective also called *case analysis*. That's follows from the
[**propositions-as-types**](https://ncatlab.org/nlab/show/propositions+as+types).

![path](/assets/latexit-images/disj-elimination.png){: width="%50" }

Finally, the induction principle for the coproduct:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15056" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="+-Ind₁"></a><a id="15063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15063" class="Module">+-Ind₁</a> <a id="15070" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="15079" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15084" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13911" class="Module">+-Def₁</a> <a id="15091" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15097" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14031" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="15101" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="15103" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Function">inl</a><a id="15106" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Function">inr</a><a id="15110" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="15112" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#5048" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a><a id="15115" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15119" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="15124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13356" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="15131" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="15137" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="15139" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="15141" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="15142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="15143" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="+-Ind₁.ind"></a><a id="15148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15148" class="Function">ind</a> <a id="15152" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15154" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15156" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15157" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15157" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15159" class="Bound">j</a><a id="15160" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15162" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15163" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15165" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15165" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15167" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15169" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="15173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15157" class="Bound">i</a><a id="15174" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15176" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15177" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15177" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15179" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15163" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14031" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="15185" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15165" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15187" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15189" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="15193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15159" class="Bound">j</a><a id="15194" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="15202" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15204" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15206" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="15208" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15163" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15211" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15213" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15177" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15217" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14166" class="Function">inl</a> <a id="15222" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15206" class="Bound">a</a><a id="15223" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="15232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15234" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="15236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15236" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="15238" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15165" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15241" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15243" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15177" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15247" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15248" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14224" class="Function">inr</a> <a id="15252" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15236" class="Bound">b</a><a id="15253" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="15262" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15264" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15265" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15163" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15271" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#14031" class="Function Operator">+</a> <a id="15273" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15165" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15274" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15276" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15278" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15177" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#15265" class="Bound">p</a>

### Exercise 1.6

<div class="exercise" id="ex-1.6">
Show that if we define $$A \times B :≡ \prod_{x:\mathbf{2}}\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbf{2}}\ (\mathcal{U}\, A\, B\, x)$$,
then we can give a definition of $$\mathsf{ind}_{A\times B}$$ for which the definitional
equalities propositionally (i.e. using equality types).
</div>

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="16060" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="×-Def₃"></a><a id="16067" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#16067" class="Module">×-Def₃</a> <a id="16074" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="16082" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="16087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13356" class="Module">𝟚-Def₁</a> <a id="16094" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="16100" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16101" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13395" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟘</a><a id="16102" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="16103" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13405" class="InductiveConstructor">𝟙</a><a id="16104" class="Symbol">;</a><a id="16105" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#13377" class="Datatype">𝟚</a><a id="16106" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16108" class="Keyword">public</a>

### Exercise 1.8

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.8">

Define multiplication and exponentiation using $$\mathsf{rec}{\mathbb{N}}$$.
Verify that $$(\mathbb{N},+,0,\times,1)$$ is a semiring using only
$$\ind{\mathbb{N}}$$.

</div>


<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>
Operation definitions:

}}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18191" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18193" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18195" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10829" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18196" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18198" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18200" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10829" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="18201" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18203" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18206" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18206" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18208" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10860" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="18214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10847" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a><a id="18218" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18220" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="18223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18223" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="18225" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18225" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18227" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18229" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18066" class="Function">multi</a> <a id="18237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18227" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="18239" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18225" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="18242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18227" class="Bound">m</a><a id="18243" class="Symbol">))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

On the other hand, a **semiring** is a type? together with two binary operators S(+,*) satisfying the following conditions:

1. Additive associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a+b)+c=a+(b+c)$$.

2. Additive commutativity: $$\prod_{a,b : S}  a+b=b+a$$.

3. Multiplicative associativity: $$\prod_{a,b,c : S} (a*b)*c=a*(b*c)$$.

4. Left and right distributivity:

$$\prod_{a,b,c : S} a*(b+c)=(a*b)+(a*c)\text{  and  } \prod_{a,b,c : S} (b+c)*a=(b*a)+(c*a).$$

</div>

### Exercise 1.9

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.9">

Define the type family $$\mathsf{Fin} : \mathbb{N} \to \mathcal{U}$$ mentioned
at the end of Section 1.3, and the dependent function $$\mathsf{fmax} :
\prod_{n:\mathbb{N}} \mathsf{Fin}(n+1)$$ mentioned in Section 1.4.
</div>

### Exercise 1.11

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.11">
Show that for any type $$A$$, we have $$\neg\neg\neg A \to \neg A$$.
</div>

A propositional logic proof using [Agda-Prop](http://github.com/jonaprieto/agda-prop)
library:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20172" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-11"></a><a id="20179" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20179" class="Module">Ex1-11</a> <a id="20186" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20194" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20199" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="20206" href="Data.PropFormula.html" class="Module">Data.PropFormula</a> <a id="20223" class="Number">1</a>

  <a id="Ex1-11.proof"></a><a id="20228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20228" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20236" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="20238" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20239" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20239" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20240" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20242" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20243" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20243" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20244" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="20254" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20256" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20239" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20258" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1657" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="20260" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20262" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20264" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20243" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20268" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#919" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊃</a> <a id="20270" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20272" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20243" class="Bound">A</a>
  <a id="20276" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20228" class="Function">proof</a> <a id="20282" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20283" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20283" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20284" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="20286" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20287" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20289" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="20295" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#3276" class="InductiveConstructor">⊃-intro</a>
      <a id="20309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20310" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
          <a id="20328" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20329" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
              <a id="20350" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20351" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20358" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20361" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20368" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20369" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20371" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20283" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="20374" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20376" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20377" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20380" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20382" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20383" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20385" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20386" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
              <a id="20406" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20407" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2276" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-intro</a>
                <a id="20431" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20432" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#2387" class="InductiveConstructor">¬-elim</a>
                  <a id="20457" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20458" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20465" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20466" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20468" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20470" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20283" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20472" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20474" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20476" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20478" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20482" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20485" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20487" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20488" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20490" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20491" class="Symbol">))</a>
                  <a id="20512" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20513" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1868" class="InductiveConstructor">weaken</a> <a id="20520" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20521" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20523" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20524" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="20526" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20527" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1706" class="InductiveConstructor">assume</a> <a id="20534" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20535" class="Argument">Γ</a> <a id="20537" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="20539" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20283" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="20541" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#1170" class="Function Operator">,</a> <a id="20543" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20545" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20547" href="Data.PropFormula.Syntax.html#966" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">¬</a> <a id="20549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20550" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20286" class="Bound">A</a><a id="20553" class="Symbol">))))))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In type theory, the term is:

$$
λ (x : ((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) (a : A) . x ((λ h : A → ⊥) . ha) :
((A → ⊥) → ⊥) → ⊥) → (A → ⊥)
$$

### Exercise 1.16

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-1.16">
Show that addition of natural numbers is commutative:
<p class="equation">
$$
\prod\limits_{i,j : \mathbb{N}}\ (i + j = j + i).
$$
</p>
</div>

Hint: by induction twice.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="20944" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Ex1-16"></a><a id="20951" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#20951" class="Module">Ex1-16</a> <a id="20958" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="20966" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#10809" class="Module">ℕ-Def</a>
  <a id="20979" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20984" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#11032" class="Module">ℕ-Ind</a>
  <a id="20992" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="20997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#17960" class="Module">Ex1-8</a> <a id="21003" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="21009" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21010" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#18001" class="Function Operator">_+_</a><a id="21013" class="Symbol">)</a>

                      <a id="21761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#21576" class="Bound">hyp₂</a><a id="21765" class="Symbol">)))</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Chapter 2

### Exercise 2.6

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.6">
Prove that if $$p : x \equiv y$$, then the function
$$(p \cdot -) : (y \equiv z) \to (x \equiv z)$$ is an equivalence.
</div>

![path-triangle](/assets/ipe-images/path-triangle.png){: width="%50" }

<div class="proof">
Solution. <br/>

To show the equivalence, it sufficies to show a function
$$g : x \equiv z \to y \equiv z$$ such that we can prove
$$ (p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$ and
$$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$.

Let's define the function $$g$$.
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
&g : x ≡ z → y ≡ z\\
&g~m~=~\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>

($$(p \cdot -) \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{x \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$m : x ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(p \cdot -) \circ g (m) &= (p \cdot -)~(g~m)\\
                        &= (p \cdot -)~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~m)\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~p~(\mathsf{sym}~p))~m\\
                        &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{x≡z}~m\\
                        &= m
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
<br/>
($$ g \circ (p \cdot -) \sim \mathsf{id}_{y \equiv z}$$):
Let be $$n : y ≡ z$$, we have,

<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
g \circ (p \cdot -) n &= g (\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= (\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~(\mathsf{trans}~p~n)\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{trans}~(\mathsf{sym}~p)~p)~n\\
                      &= \mathsf{trans}~\mathsf{refl}_{y ≡ z}~n\\
                      &= n.
\end{align*}
$$
</p>

</div>


### Exercise 2.10

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.10">
Prove that ∑-types are associative, in that for any $$A : \mathcal{U}$$
and families $$B : A  \to U$$ and $$C : \sum_{(x : A)} B(x) \to \mathcal{U}$$,
we have
<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \simeq \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
</div>

<div class="proof" id="proof-2.10">
Solution.<br/>
We can prove that the following functions $$f$$ and $$g$$ are inverses.

<p class="equation">
$$\sum\limits_{(x : A)} \sum\limits_{(y : B(x))} C((x,y)) \overset{f}{\underset{g}{\rightleftarrows}} \sum\limits_{p : \sum_{x:A} B(x)} C(p)$$.
</p>
defined by $$f(a,b,c) :\equiv ((a,b),c)$$ and $$g(z,c) :\equiv (\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)$$.<br/>
Indeed,
<p class="equation">
$$
\begin{align*}
(f \circ g) (z, c) &:\equiv f (g (z,c))\\
&:\equiv f\,(\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z, c)\\
&:\equiv ((\mathsf{proj}_1 z,\mathsf{proj}_{2} z), c)
\end{align*}
$$
</p>
</div>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.f-g"></a><a id="24862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24862" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="24866" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24868" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="24870" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24871" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24871" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24873" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24875" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24878" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24881" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24881" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24885" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24871" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24887" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24889" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24892" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24894" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24895" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="24897" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4976" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24871" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24903" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24881" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24905" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24907" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="24910" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="24920" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24923" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24925" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4976" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24930" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4976" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24932" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24871" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24934" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24881" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24935" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24895" class="Bound">C</a><a id="24938" class="Symbol">)</a>
        <a id="24948" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24950" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24561" class="Function">f</a> <a id="24952" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24953" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="24955" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24957" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24871" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24958" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24960" class="Argument">B</a> <a id="24962" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24881" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24965" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="24967" class="Argument">C</a> <a id="24969" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24895" class="Bound">C</a><a id="24972" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24975" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24702" class="Function">g</a> <a id="24977" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24923" class="Bound">x</a><a id="24978" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24980" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#766" class="Datatype Operator">≡</a> <a id="24982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24923" class="Bound">x</a>
  <a id="24986" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24862" class="Function">f-g</a> <a id="24990" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#24990" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24992" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24994" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#814" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>

  <a id="Σ-Fun₁.g-f"></a><a id="25002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25002" class="Function">g-f</a> <a id="25006" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25008" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="25010" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25011" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25013" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25015" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25018" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25020" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25021" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25023" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25011" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25027" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25029" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25032" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="25034" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="25035" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25035" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="25037" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#4976" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="25041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25011" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25043" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25021" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25045" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25047" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a><a id="25050" class="Symbol">}</a>
        <a id="25060" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-04-08-hott-exercises.md %}{% raw %}#25063" ### Exercise 2.13

<div class="exercise" id="exercise-2.13">
Show that $$(2 \simeq 2) \simeq 2$$.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Solution.<br/>

The following text is from [jdoughertyii](https://github.com/jdoughertyii/hott-exercises/blob/master/Ch02.v).<br/>
The result essentially says that $$2$$ is equivalent to itself in two ways:
the identity provides one equivalence, and negation gives the other.  So we
first define these.  $$\mathsf{id}_{2}$$ is its own quasi-inverse; we have
$$\mathsf{id}_{2} \circ \mathsf{id}_{2} \equiv \mathsf{id}_{2}$$, so $$\mathsf{id}_{2}
\circ \mathsf{id}_{2}
\sim \mathsf{id}_{2}$$ easily.  $$\lnot$$ is also its own quasi-inverse, since for
any $$x$$, $$\lnot\lnot x = x$$.
To show the result, we need to map $$\mathsf{id}_{2}$$ and $$\lnot$$ onto $$2$$ is
a quasi-invertible way.  But we need to define this map on all of $$2
\simeq 2$$.  So for any $$h : 2\simeq 2$$, let $$f(h) = h(0_{2})$$,
and define $$g : 2 \to (2 \simeq 2)$$ by

$$
  g(0_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2}
  \qquad\qquad
  g(1_{2}) = \lnot
$$

To show that these are quasi-inverses,
note first that whatever else is the case, an equivalence
$$2 \simeq 2$$ can't be a constant function, which we can prove by a case
analysis.  Each of $$f(0_{2})$$ and $$f(1_{2})$$ is in $$2$$, so it is
either $$0_{2}$$ or $$1_{2}$$.  So we have the cases:
 - $$f(0_{2}) = f(1_{2})$$, in which case we can apply $$f^{-1}$$ to either side to get a contradiction, or
 - $$f(0_{2}) = \lnot f(1_{2})$$. In which case we have the result
Showing that $$f \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{2}$$ is easy, since we can do it by
cases.  We have

$$\begin{align*}
  f(g(0_{2})) &= f(\mathsf{id}_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2}(0_{2}) = 0_{2}
  \\
  f(g(1_{2})) &= f(\lnot) = \lnot 0_{2} = 1_{2}
\end{align*}%
$$

For the other direction, suppose that $$h : 2 \simeq 2$$ and that
function extensionality holds.
$$h(0_{2})$$ is either $$0_{2}$$ or $$1_{2}$$.  If the first, then
because $$h$$ isn't constant we have $$h(1_{2}) = \lnot h(0_{2}) =
1_{2}$$, hence $$h = \mathsf{id}_{2}$$.  Furthermore,
$$
  g(f(h)) = g(h(0_{2})) = g(0_{2}) = \mathsf{id}_{2} = h
$$
The same argument works for the other case.  So $$f$$ is an equivalence, and
$$(2 \simeq 2) \simeq 2$$.

</div>

### Exercise 2.14

<div class="exercise">

  Suppose we add to type theory <a
  href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=IlfQjWqrK6I">the equality reflection
  rule</a> which says that if there is an element $$p : \mathsf{Id}(x,y) $$,
  then in fact $$ x :\equiv y$$. Prove that for any $$p : \mathsf{Id}(x,x)$$ we
  have $$p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_x$$.

  <p class="equation">
  $$
    \begin{prooftree}
    \AxiomC{$\vdash p : \mathsf{Id}(x, y)$}
    \RightLabel{$\mathsf{Eq}$}
    \UnaryInfC{$\vdash x \equiv y.$}
    \end{prooftree}
  $$
  </p>

</div>

<div class="proof">
  Proof.<br/>
  We first fix the type of $$\mathsf{refl}_x$$ in order to apply effectively
  path induction.<br/>

  <p class="equation">
    $$
    \begin{prooftree}
    \AxiomC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ p : x = y$}
    \RightLabel{$\mathsf{Eq}$}
    \UnaryInfC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ x ≡ y$}
    \AxiomC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ \mathsf{refl}_x : x = x$}
    \BinaryInfC{$x : A, y : A, p : x = y ⊢ \mathsf{refl}_x : x = y.$}
    \end{prooftree}
    $$
  </p>

  Now, $$\mathsf{refl}_x$$ and $$p : x = y$$ in the formulation of path induction
  are well-typed. Therefore, by path induction, we show that
  $$\mathsf{Id}(p,\mathsf{refl_{x}})$$. Let be $$x : A$$ and $$C :\equiv
  \prod_{y : A} \prod_{p : x \equiv y }\ p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_{x}$$.
  It sufficies to show and inhabitant of $$C(x, \mathsf{refl}_{x})$$, and this is
  $$\mathsf{refl}_{\mathsf{refl}_x} : \mathsf{refl}_x = \mathsf{refl}_x$$.
  By the equation reflection rule, since we have an inhabitant of $$p \equiv
  \mathsf{refl}_x$$, we conclude these terms are judgemental equal,i.e., $$p \equiv \mathsf{refl}_x$$.
</div>

### Exercise 2.17

<div class="exercise">
<ul>
  <li> Show that if $$A \simeq A$$  and $$B \simeq B'$$, then $$(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$$. </li>
  <li> Give two proofs of this fact, one using univalence and one not using it, and show that the two proofs are equal.</li>
  <li> Formulate and prove analogous results for the other type formers: $$\Sigma$$, $$\to$$, $$\Pi$$, and $$+$$. </li>
</ul>
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
- Assuming univalence.
<br/>
$$
\begin{prooftree}
\AxiomC{$f : A \simeq A$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{ua}$}
\UnaryInfC{$A =_{\mathcal{U}} A$}
\AxiomC{$g : B \simeq B'$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{ua}$}
\UnaryInfC{$B =_{\mathcal{U}} B'$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{pair=}$}
\BinaryInfC{$(A\times B) =_{\mathcal{U}} (A'\times B')$}
\RightLabel{$\mathsf{idtoequiv}$}
\UnaryInfC{$(A\times B) \simeq (A'\times B')$}
\end{prooftree}
$$

- Without using univalence, it is easy to prove
that the function $$h$$ defined as follows gives us the
equivalence that we are looking for.

$$
\begin{align*}
&h : (A\times B) \to (A'\times B')\\
&h (a , b) = (f\, a, g\, b).
\end{align*}
$$

With the inverse:

$$
\begin{align*}
&h^{-1} : (A'\times B') \to (A\times B)\\
&h^{-1} (a , b) = (f^{-1}\, a, g^{-1}\, b).
\end{align*}
$$

To prove these proofs are equal it is sufficies to
show these underlyding functions are equal.


</div>

## Chapter 3

To solve the following exercises, let us recall a few things:

- The *set* definition in HoTT:

A type $$A$$ is a **set** if for all $$x, y : A$$ and
all $$p, q : x \equiv y$$, we have $$ p \equiv q$$. In a proposition
we have

$$
\mathsf{isSet}(A) :\equiv \prod\limits_{(x,y : A)}\prod\limits_{(p,q : x \equiv y)} (p \equiv q).
$$

- The type for equivalence from $$A$$ to $$B$$

$$
  (A \simeq B) :\equiv \sum\limits_{f : A \to B} \mathsf{isequiv}(f),
$$

where

$$
\mathsf{isequiv(f)} :\equiv
  \left (\sum\limits_{g : B \to A} (f \circ g \sim \mathsf{id}_{B})\right) \times
  \left (\sum\limits_{h : B \to A} (h \circ f \sim \mathsf{id}_{A})\right)
$$

- The homotopy concept:

Let $$f , g : \prod\limits_{(x:A)} P(x)$$ be two sections of a
type family $$P : A \to \mathcal{U}$$. A **homotopy** from $$f$$ to $$g$$
is a dependent function of type

$$
(f \sim g) :\equiv \prod\limits_{x : A} (f(x) \equiv g(x)).
$$

### Exercise 3.1

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A\simeq B$$ and $$A$$ is a set, then so is $$B$$.
</div>


<div class="proof" id="proof-3.1" markdown="1" >
Proof 1.<br/>
Let be $$x,y : B$$ and $$p : x \equiv_{B} y$$ and $$q : x \equiv_{B} y$$.
We need to prove $$ p \equiv q$$.<br/>
Since $$A\simeq B$$ then there is a function $$f : A \to B$$ and some
$$g : B \to A$$ such that $$f \circ g \sim id_{B}$$.
Using this function $$g$$ over the path $$p$$ we get
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} p : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
We do the same but this time over the path $$q$$, that is,
$$\mathsf{ap}_{g} q : g x \equiv_{A} g y$$.
Because of $$A$$ is a set, we have a new path called
$$m :\mathsf{ap}_{g} p \equiv_{gx \equiv_{A} gy} \mathsf{ap}_{g} q$$. <br/>

Now, an action over this path $$m$$
using the function $$\mathsf{ap}_{f} : x \equiv_{A} y \to f x \equiv_{B} f y$$
will give us


$$
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m :
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q).
$$


By the lemmas in Chapter 2, we do the following reasoning:

$$
\begin{align*}
(\mathsf{ap}_{f}) (\mathsf{ap}_{g} p) \equiv (\mathsf{ap}_{f})  (\mathsf{ap}_{g} q) &=
  \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{f \circ g} q\\
  &=(\text{transporting by using} f \sim g)\\
  &=\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} p \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{id}_{B}} q\\
  &=p \equiv q.
\end{align*}
$$

Then, we have the inhabitant, $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{ap}_{f}} m : p \equiv q$$.
</div>

### Exercise 3.2

<div class="exercise">
Prove that if $$A$$ and $$B$$ are sets, then so is $$A+B$$.
</div>

To solve this exercise, we should take a look of some results from Chapter 2,
Section 2.12.

<div class="proof" id="proof-3.2" markdown="1">
Proof.<br/>

Let be $$x, y : A + B$$, and paths $$p : x \equiv y$$, $$q : x \equiv
y$$. Let's get a path $$p \equiv q$$.  We proceed by case analysis. If
$$x :\equiv \mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, for
some $$a, b : A$$ then $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p : a
\equiv_{A} b$$ and $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q : a \equiv_{A}
b$$.

Since $$A$$ is a set, there is a path between these last two terms,
this is, $$m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p \equiv
\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q$$.  Now, an action over this path
$$m$$ using the $$\mathsf{inl}$$ function give us:
$$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}} m : \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv \mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} q)$$.<br/>

By path algebra we have $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
m : p \equiv q$$ since $$\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}}
(\mathsf{ap}_{\mathsf{inl}^{-1}} p) \equiv p$$.<br/> Following the
same reasoning, we prove the case $$x :\equiv \mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y
:\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$.  For the latest cases, $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inl} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inr} b$$ and $$x :\equiv
\mathsf{inr} a$$ and $$y :\equiv \mathsf{inl} b$$, we use the
encode-decode method to derive a proof term for 𝟘 from
$$p$$ and $$q$$. Then, we may conclude anything we wish, that is, $$p
\equiv q$$.
</div>


### Exercise 3.4

<div class="exercise">
Show that $$A$$ is a mere proposition if and only
if $$A\to A$$ is contractible.
</div>

<div class="proof" markdown="1">
Proof. <br/>
- We must to show an inhabitant of the following type:

$$
\mathsf{isProp}(A) \to \sum\limits_{f : A \to A}\, \prod\limits_{g : A \to A } f = g.
$$

This is my proposed term:

$$
t :\equiv λ \mathsf{Aprop} \to (\mathsf{id}_{A}, λ (g : A \to A) \to \mathsf{funext} (\lambda (x : A) \to \mathsf{Aprop}~(\mathsf{id}~x)~(g~x)).
$$

- If $$A → A$$ is contractible, all functions in this type are equal,
then in particular given $$x, y : A$$, the constant functions $$f(w) \equiv x$$
and $$g(w) \equiv y$$ are equal. Then, $$\mathsf{happly} (f =_{A \to A} g, w) : x = y$$.
Therefore $$A$$ is a mere proposition.

</div>
